It was resolved to keep it for discussion at the next meeting. (6) The report of the Legal Committee of the Legislative Yuan, together with the Military Committee, on the review and amendment of the organization law of the Military Council. It was resolved to pass it.

Regulations on the Organization of Provincial and Municipal Offices for National Assembly Representative Elections

The National Government promulgated the Regulations on the Organization of Provincial and Municipal Offices for National Assembly Representative Elections on the 21st. The original text is as follows:

▲Article 1: Each provincial election supervisor and each municipal election supervisor shall establish a National Assembly Representative Election Office in a certain province or city to handle election affairs. The aforementioned election offices shall be directed and supervised by the General Election Office of National Assembly Representatives.

▲Article 2: The General Election Office of National Assembly Representatives may send personnel to guide the provincial and municipal offices when necessary.

Article 3: Each provincial election office shall direct and supervise the counties in handling election matters and may send personnel to guide them when necessary.

▲Article 4: The following matters must be promptly reported to the General Election Office of National Assembly Representatives by each provincial and municipal election office: (1) The organization and history of each qualified electoral group; (2) The names and resumes of the election supervisors, ballot counting administrators, and voting administrators of each group; (3) The investigation and punishment of electoral fraud stipulated in Article 17 of the National Assembly Representative Election Law; (4) The determination of re-elections stipulated in Article 21 of the National Assembly Representative Election Law.

▲Article 5: Each provincial and municipal election office shall establish the following three groups, and each group may establish several sections to manage affairs: (1) General Affairs Group, responsible for document accounting, general affairs, and matters not belonging to other groups; (2) Review Group, responsible for reviewing the qualifications of various groups and voters and candidates; (3) Guidance Group, responsible for guiding election procedures.

▲Article 6: The affairs of each provincial election office shall be managed by the chief election supervisor of each province, who shall direct and supervise subordinate staff, county election supervisors, and personnel handling election affairs in various groups. The affairs of each municipal election office shall be managed by the chief election supervisor of each city, who shall direct and supervise subordinate staff and personnel handling election affairs in various groups.

▲Article 7: Each provincial and municipal election office shall have one chief secretary and three to five secretaries, who shall handle affairs under the command of the chief election supervisor or election supervisor.

▲Article 8: Each group in the provincial and municipal election offices shall have one group leader, concurrently held by a secretary, and each section shall have one section leader, several clerks, and several secretaries, who shall handle affairs under the command of their superiors.

▲Article 9: The personnel in the preceding two articles shall be transferred from various agencies. The positions they hold shall be selected and assigned by the chief election supervisor or election supervisor.

▲Article 10: The date of establishment and the names and resumes of the staff of each provincial and municipal election office must be reported to the General Election Office of National Assembly Representatives for record.

▲Article 11: Each provincial and municipal election office shall be abolished after the election is completed.

▲Article 12: These regulations shall come into effect from the date of promulgation.

Record of the Inauguration of the Shanxi Provincial Committee

Taiyuan Communication: The newly appointed Acting Chairman of the Shanxi Provincial Government, Shang Zhen, and committee members Chang Bingyi, Zhang Weiqing, Guo Baoqing, and others, held a swearing-in ceremony at the Provincial Government Auditorium at 10:00 AM yesterday. The Secretariat of the Provincial Government specially issued a notice the night before, requesting various agencies and organizations to send representatives to observe the ceremony.

(1) Shang Zhen (2) Miao Peicheng (3) Zhang Weiqing

(4) Guo Baoqing (5) Chang Bingyi

Approximately 300 to 400 representatives attended. The venue was decorated in an extremely solemn manner, with tables and chairs in the center and a bouquet of flowers. The seats for guests were filled on both the east and west sides, and the military band stood in the courtyard. When the clock struck ten, Shang, accompanied by the Central Supervisor Miao Peicheng, committee members Chang Bingyi, Guo Baoqing, Zhang Weiqing, and others, walked from the Provincial Government Reception Hall to the auditorium. After entering the auditorium, the military band played loudly. Shang and Miao were all dressed in ordinary formal attire. After taking their seats, Miao sat in the center, with Shang and the committee members arranged on both sides. After the ceremony, Shang read the oath on behalf of everyone, saying: "I solemnly swear that I will abide by the will of the Premier, obey the laws of the Party and the country, be loyal and diligent in my duties, I will never waste a penny, use a person wrongly, and I will never engage in corruption or accept bribes. If I violate this oath, I am willing to accept the most severe punishment. This I swear." Next, Miao Peicheng delivered a speech, saying in summary: "Chairman and committee members, representatives, today is the day when the Shanxi Provincial Government is reorganized and Chairman Shang and the committee members are sworn into office. I have been sent by the Central Government to supervise the oath-taking ceremony. I have three feelings about participating in this meeting, which I would like to present for the reference of the Chairman and committee members: (1) Shanxi is in the aftermath of a major war, and the scars have not yet healed. Although it has been several months, it has still not been able to recover. The voices of the disaster-stricken people in various places continue to reach our ears. At the time of the establishment of the new government, it is hoped that local relief will be handled quickly and social order will be stabilized. (2) Now is the period of political tutelage, and local self-government is extremely important. Now that the provincial government is reorganized, I hope to work hard to guide local self-government so that the people have the ability to govern themselves. (3) Shanxi has stubbornly clung to old habits for the past ten years, and many systems and regulations are no longer applicable today. I hope that after the reorganization of the provincial government, we can start anew and completely eliminate all the bad habits and bad regulations that are outdated and stagnant." Next, Hu Boyue, the representative of the Provincial Party Department, and Yang Derong, the representative of the Municipal Party Department, delivered speeches one after another, both hoping to show determination and perseverance to do things for the people and to promote local self-government. Finally, Shang Zhen, on behalf of the committee members, gave a reply, saying: "Central Supervisor, representatives of the Provincial and Municipal Party Departments, representatives from all walks of life, comrades, I am honored and grateful for your presence and guidance today. From now on, we will respectfully abide by the Party's doctrine and program, the Premier's instructions and teachings, and the various points instructed by the Central Supervisor and the representatives, and strive to realize them with twelve points of enthusiasm and effort. We will also abide by the Central Government's laws, be mindful of the people's suffering, eliminate all the malpractices of the past government, and do our best to seek welfare for the people of the province. As for the detailed methods and implementation procedures, we will formulate a comprehensive plan after taking office so that we can implement it. We are but thin and weak in talent and strength, and we still hope that you comrades will provide guidance at any time so that we can follow and not be mistaken. This is especially what we hope for." After Shang finished his reply, he went to the outside of the auditorium with everyone and took a photo together before dispersing. After supervising the oath-taking ceremony, Miao Peicheng went directly to the station and took the Zhengtai train at noon to leave Bing and return to Beijing to report. The reason why the committee members were so eager to take office was because Miao had to leave Jin that day. After Shang and the committee members took office, they issued a telegram of assuming office. The original text is as follows: Urgent: Central Party Headquarters, National Government, Presidents of each Yuan, various departments, various committee members, various provincial and municipal governments, various provincial and municipal party headquarters, various legal entities, various newspapers, all for reference: According to the National Government's order of January 31, appointing Shang Zhen, Zhang Jixin, Chang Bingyi, Feng Sizhi, Qiu Zengyi, Zhang Weiqing, Guo Maiqing, Li Shangren, and Hu Yiling as members of the Shanxi Provincial Government this order; appointing Shang Zhen concurrently as Chairman of the Shanxi Provincial Government this order; appointing Shang Zhen concurrently as Director of the Department of Civil Affairs of the Shanxi Provincial Government, Zhang Jixin concurrently as Director of the Department of Finance of the Shanxi Provincial Government, Feng Sizhi concurrently as Director of the Department of Education of the Shanxi Provincial Government, Qiu Zengyi concurrently as Director of the Department of Construction of the Shanxi Provincial Government, and Chang Bingyi concurrently as Director of the Department of Agriculture and Industry of the Shanxi Provincial Government, this order, etc. In accordance with this, we took the oath of office at 9:00 AM today. We are unworthy of such a new mandate and fear that the times are difficult and the responsibility is heavy. We hope that you will give us advice from time to time so that we can follow and not be mistaken. We pray without end. Shang Zhen, Zhang Jixin, Chang Bingyi, Feng Sizhi, Qiu Zengyi, Zhang Weiqing, Guo Baoqing, Li Shangren, and Hu Yiling respectfully request deletion. (February 16)

Wang Jinyu Establishes Bandit Suppression Headquarters in Nanchang

▲Has Sent Chief of Staff to Nanchang to Make Arrangements

Nanchang Communication: Wang Jinyu, Bandit Suppression Commissioner for the borders of Hunan, Hubei, and Jiangxi, has sent his Chief of Staff Qi Xiangchen to Jiangxi to meet with He Yingqin to request instructions on the bandit suppression strategy for the borders of the three provinces and to report on the progress of the bandit suppression. After arriving in the province, Qi visited He at the headquarters and then went to visit Commander-in-Chief Lu at his residence in Beitan, and also visited Mayor Gong at the Municipal Government, preparing to establish a three-province bandit suppression headquarters in the provincial capital. Wang Jinyu will not come to Nanchang to command everything until the arrangements are in order. Because the joint suppression by the three provinces must first clear out the Jiangxi bandits. It is reported that the 54th Division, commanded by Hao Mengling, is currently stationed in Xiushui, and Hao has also taken office as Chairman of the Xiushui Bandit Suppression Zone Committee. The 43rd Division, commanded by Guo Huazong, has arrived in the area of Wanzai, Lianhua, and Anfu, and has established contact with friendly forces in eastern Hunan and western Jiangxi. The 47th Division is also advancing towards the borders of Jiangxi, Hunan, and Hubei. In the future, part of Chen Cheng's division will also come to Jiangxi to join the bandit suppression. Therefore, the bandit communists in Jiangxi can be expected to be cleared in a short period of time. (February 19)

Li Mingzhong and Others Request the Abolition of Additional Security Fees in Henan

Li Mingzhong, Liu Zhenhua, and others sent a telegram to Chairman Liu of Henan, saying: "Chairman Liu Jingfu, with respect. We believe that the way to govern well is to prioritize a sufficient army with sufficient food, and the way to stop chaos is to emphasize both nurturing and protecting the people. In recent years, the central government, with the intention of relieving suffering, sent troops to suppress violence and save the people. Great chaos has been quelled repeatedly, and the country is unified. Repeated proclamations have been issued to allow the people to rest, and benevolent words and benefits have been widely spread, admired by all. Moreover, Henan Province has suffered from frequent years of drought and has been at the center of successive wars. The granaries are empty, and scars are everywhere. Your Excellency deeply cares for the people's suffering and vigorously plans for pacification. The remaining breaths are gradually reviving, and we are fortunate to see the day of yearning for good governance. Harsh taxes are pending, especially at a time when they are on the verge of death. Recently, we have seen the provincial government's security team measures, establishing a headquarters in the provincial capital and forming four regiments, requiring more than 200,000 yuan in monthly expenses. A security fee of 60 cents is added to each tael of land tax, implemented from the 20th year [of the Republic] and extended to six districts in the province. The expenses for the security teams in each district are still raised locally, amounting to no less than several million yuan. According to the Ministry of Finance's circular, the surtax on land should not exceed one times the regular tax. In some counties in Henan Province, it exceeds several times, and some report the correct amount but still arbitrarily apportion the taxes. This time, the Department of Finance telegraphed instructions to the counties to separately review and reduce the additional amounts for education, construction, public security, police, self-government, and local militias, and to increase the security fees separately, hoping to avoid the name of exceeding the tax. Although the wording does not violate the Ministry's order, in reality

Page 10

, it greatly increases the burden. Now that political tutelage has begun, the key to local administration is to reflect and catch up. If the old amount of local fees is reduced due to the new increase in security fees, judging from the principles of things, it is not proper. Moreover, the education, construction, public security, self-government, local militias, and other expenses of each county have fixed amounts and regular uses, which cannot be reduced by empty words. Ultimately, it is feared that the old ones will not be reduced, and the new ones will be permanently added, causing the small people to suffer skinning pain. Furthermore, speaking in terms of the nature of the local militias and the security teams, the local militias are the people's self-defense force, and the security teams are the provincial government's force for maintaining public order. Therefore, the expenses of the local militias should be borne by the people, and the expenses of the security teams should be provided by the provincial treasury according to Article 19 of the organizational regulations promulgated by the central government. The war responsibilities and military expenses are planned in an orderly manner. If the funds for the local militias are diverted for security fees, it is like cutting feet to fit shoes. If the increase in security fees causes a heavy burden on the people, it is like drinking poison to quench thirst. However, if the government intends to concentrate military force and achieve the effect of command and control, it can be said that although the local area increases its burden, the government still receives its effect, and it can also be said that although the people increase their huge burden, they still obtain the price of security. However, we, those in charge, based on internal information, believe that this is not the case. Tracing back to the time when Governor Zhao was in office during the 10th year of the Republic, he formed dozens of battalions of local patrol teams, with salaries taken from the local area and soldiers forcibly taken from the local militias. However, during the Zhili-Fengtian War, they abandoned their armor and dragged their weapons, collapsing and scattering like a warehouse. They were not enough to maintain anything in an emergency. Last year, Feng occupied Henan Province and forcibly formed local militia armies in various counties in an attempt to increase his personal power. In the end, the militia disintegrated, and the fog and smoke dissipated. A crowd of rabble-rousers instantly turned into nothing. The local militia is essentially a self-defense group, not a combat force. The salaries and weapons of the local militia are tools for protecting the people and should not be used as weapons of war. To covet the false name of centralized power is to receive the real disaster of making enemies. The repeated mistakes and lessons are not far away. Zhenhua and others belong to the common people and have more direct observations. For the sake of the provincial government's maintenance of the local area and for the sake of reducing the people's suffering in Henan, rather than taking the risk of cutting flesh to treat sores, it is better to plan for bending chimneys and moving firewood. We dare to offer our humble opinions and attach our loyal advice. Our public pain is held in our arms, and we hope for your understanding. We earnestly request that you issue a general order to all counties to abolish the additional security fees to alleviate the people's difficulties. If it is deemed that security urgently needs to be arranged and the people cannot bear any more burdens, it seems appropriate to adjust the existing budget within the provincial treasury and find other ways to benefit both security and alleviate difficulties. We respectfully telegraph our sincere intentions and hope for your consideration. Brothers Li Mingzhong, Ji Hongchang, Liang Guanying, and Liu Zhenhua bow with seals. Also, a telegram to Chief of Staff Liu: "Chief of Staff Liu Shishang, with respect. Parting at Dongmen has been toiling. Recently, we heard that the Department of Finance of the provincial government issued a general order to add 60 cents of security fees to the land tax in the 20th year and remit the full amount to the province. In addition, the expenses for the security teams under the jurisdiction of the six districts are still to be raised separately by the local areas. Our region has suffered from frequent years of drought, the people are poor and the wealth is exhausted, and the survivors after the calamity cannot bear this. We have witnessed the suffering and speak out for the people. We have telegraphed Chairman Jingfu, earnestly requesting that he consider the people's hardships and find other ways. We hope for your understanding. We believe that the establishment of the security teams is originally intended to maintain local public order. According to the regulations promulgated by the central government, the expenses should be provided by the provincial treasury. If this huge amount heavily burdens the people, we sincerely fear that security will not be achieved and the people's lives will be exhausted. We have no choice but to take this step of shouting out. Our brother is deeply concerned about his homeland, and his heart for loving his hometown is closely related and even more urgent than ours. We hope that you will explain in detail to all colleagues in charge and strive to mediate before Chairman Jingfu to express our humble sincerity. Then, the tens of millions of dying people in our Henan will feel the boundless grace of a great man. We offer our sincerity with urgency. Brothers Li Mingzhong, Ji Hongchang, Liang Guanying, and Liu Zhenhua bow with seals."

The Loss of Haiyuan Pavilion's Collection of Books to Bandit Dens

Jinan Correspondence: A portion of the Haiyuan Pavilion collection of books belonging to the Yang family in Liaocheng was transported to Jinan and preserved by the stepmother of the book owner, Yang Jingfu. Another portion was transported to the Chang residence of Lao Zhi in Tianjin. The other portion was looted by the bandit gang of Xue Chuanfeng and Wang Jinfeng when they occupied Liaocheng. It has now been scattered to Baoding, and the ones sold are not included. As for the portion transported to Jinan, the Department of Education has repeatedly negotiated with them and proposed three methods to preserve it. However, the old Mrs. Yang did not trust the government and repeatedly made excuses and delayed, and the negotiations have come to no results. Yang Jingfu, on the other hand, claimed to be ill in Tianjin and did not come to Jinan. Therefore, this matter is currently at a standstill. However, it is heard that twelve kinds have been sold to the Japanese for 80,000 yuan. In addition to the Song edition of Meng Dongye's Collection and the Liao family's Liuzhou Collection from the Shicai Hall, there is also a Song edition of Zhuangzi, which is also a unique copy in the country. The Liuzhou Collection was only priced at 8,000 yuan, which can be said to be of good quality and low price. Recently, Rong Guangxing, the brigade commander of the 87th Brigade of the 29th Division of the Third Route Army, was suppressing bandits in Boping and discovered the Haiyuan Pavilion collection of books in the bandit's residence. However, it was already badly damaged. The brigade immediately telegraphed a report to the province, which stated: "On the 15th of this month, the commander of our brigade personally led the entire Second Regiment and the pistol team to various counties for guerrilla warfare. It was reported that in Suoti, Boping, there were bandit leaders Dafengzi Wang Erbiandan who were summoning bandit troops, hoping to disturb the local area. This bandit once served as a battalion commander under Wang Guanjun. When the Wang bandits occupied Liaocheng, they stole many treasures from the Yang residence. We immediately secretly ordered the pistol team to surround Suoti and the bandit's residence at dawn. Led by the villagers, they entered the courtyard to search. Unexpectedly, the bandits had already heard the news and fled. We arrested their father and more than ten suspects and escorted them back to the brigade headquarters for strict interrogation. At the same time, we found several pages of calligraphy and painting in the courtyard, which were indeed owned by the Yang residence, but they were badly damaged. It is heard that the valuable ones had already been transported elsewhere. On the 16th, the pistol team went to the West Civilization District and captured Pang Yuchun, a major bandit from Liaocheng. On the 17th, they closed the city gates again, checked the household registrations, and acted swiftly in various counties, causing great shock. The bandits have already disappeared, and at the same time, we jointly issued a notice with the county magistrates to appease the people, and the people's hearts are greatly stabilized. Special report, Chief of Staff's Office of the 87th Brigade, Qiaoyin." (20th day)

Local Correspondence

Songjiang

Joint Suppression of Bandits by Land and Naval Forces, Police, and Army, Ji The bandit Tai Bao Ah Shu is scattered throughout the towns of Songjiang and Jinshan. The troops stationed in Songjiang have repeatedly dispatched teams to suppress them. However, the area has many river branches, and the bandits and villagers wear the same clothing, making it difficult to distinguish between good and bad. On the 18th, at 12:00 PM, the land and naval forces, police, and army were each divided into a column and set off in six routes. Zhang Ruyu, the battalion commander of the Fifth Division, Bai, the battalion commander of the security team, Fan, the captain of the water police, Ren, the company commander of the Fifth Division, Tan, the captain of the Jinshan water patrol, Yang Shi, the inspector of the Songjiang Public Security Bureau and the secret service chief of the Jinshan Clearing Office, and Fan, the squad leader, each led elite troops and set off from their stationed locations. They were to gather at Xinmiao to conduct a major search. The Zhejiang Pinghu also sent a security team to come and join them. In the early stages, the small ports were sealed off. From 12:00 PM onwards, until dawn, the sound of gunfire continued from all directions. In this campaign, Tai Bao Ah Shu and others had already fled Xinmiao several hours earlier. It is rumored that they had fallen into the sea to escape. Only the third route led by Captain Tan, Detective Yang, and Squad Leader Fan set off from Zhang and arrived at Kongjiaque. They caught a glimpse of a flash of electricity and searched forward without success. They turned to Langxia and arrived at Majiahui at 5:00 AM and intercepted

two bandits, Liu Badi and Gao Erer, who confessed to the location of the hidden ransom slips. They were escorted to the Ma Jinxiang family and rescued seven hostages who had been kidnapped from Xinhuang. Five hostages were also found in the Ma Ahe family. The bandits watching the hostages had all escaped and were lying on the river beach. They were searched and captured by Detective Yang, Captain Tan, and others, totaling seven people. Among them was Jin Qisheng, the younger brother of Jin Fei, and Gao Erer, Gao Ersan, Liu Atao, and others who were the most vicious. The various routes then gathered, and the third route brought the hostages and bandits back to Zhang. After interrogation by Battalion Commander Zhang and others, Jin Qisheng confessed that he was 24 years old, from Qianwei, and had served as a police officer. Last June, he followed the Tai Bao Ah Shu gang to rob Jinjiazhuang and other places. On the fourth day of the eleventh month, he followed Xu Tianmin (Tai Bao Ah Shu's younger brother), Wang Meimei (Pig

Ah Mei), Lu Yaosheng, and others and obtained nineteen hostages. Tai Bao Ah Shu took three, and Wang Meimei took the rest to wait for ransom. The day before,

they gathered many people in Mahui to kidnap Xie Yuchun from Jiangzhuang and six others.

According to Gao Erer, who was also from Qianwei, he was rowing boats for Ah Bao Taishu in December. The Shen Youche kidnapping case was planned at Huxiao Bridge behind Liujiayan Bridge. The other criminals all confessed without denying. Jin Qisheng, Gao Erer, and two others were executed by firing squad at Zhangyan Yaotou on the 20th. Liu Badi and the other three were scheduled to be executed by firing squad in Zhangyan today. An empty boat and three rifles seized from the bandits in Xinmiao have been brought back. It is reported that the bandits abandoned their boats and landed to escape because they were surrounded by land and naval forces, police, and army and the river ports were sealed off. The twelve hostages rescued were Jiang Jusheng, Chen Guofu, Yao Shaozhou, Jin Pan

, Xu Chunlin, Xu Huiren, Xu Shaogui, Wang Yaoshan, Zhu Fukang, Zheng Lizhang, Lu Fengqing, and Dai Chenshi, who were businessmen. Ten of them returned to Song today and took a car back to He, and the other two had to wait for their families to come and claim them.

The Kidnapping Case of the Zhu Family in Wuku is Resolved The Zhu Anda family of Zhangcunbang, Wuku Thirty-Eight Tu was kidnapped by bandits at the end of the lunar year. Anda's children and a nephew were kidnapped, and there was no news for a long time. The family was anxious. It is now known that all those kidnapped were escaped from the Qingpu Tangbian on New Year's Eve and arrived safely at home that night. The whole family was happy.

Qingpu

The Kidnapping of Fang Baolong Demands a Ransom of 100,000 After Fang Baolong and his grandson, residents of Xiao Jing, Sian Bridge, were kidnapped by bandits at the end of January, it is now known that the family received a letter from the bandits demanding a ransom of 100,000 yuan. The contact location is Liuhe Town, which belongs to Taicang County. It is said that the Fang family has used all its wealth, which is less than 100,000. It is unknown how to redeem them.

Suzhou

Frequent Bandit Alarms in Wu and Wu Jiang The areas of Luli and Wu Jiang have had bandit gangs arriving from Zhejiang province last night. There are 30 or 40 bandit ships, intending to take advantage of the New Year to rob the town when the defenses are weak. The water police team stationed there detected this and dispatched a team to block them. The bandits still fled back to Zhejiang province.

Wuxi

The Sentencing of Zhou Runshi and Others Zhou Runshi, a police inspector of the Civil Affairs Department, was staying with Zhou Xingzhen, the concubine of Shen Xiang, in Wuxi. Shen presented a complaint, and the county government transferred Zhou Runshi and others to the county court. Prosecutor Zhou opened the court and acquitted Zhou Runshi and others. According to the Law on Violations of Police Regulations, they were sent to the Public Security Bureau for sentencing. As the fixed period was not yet over, they were still detained. Yesterday, the fixed period expired, and the court sent a letter to the county government. The county government then issued a letter to the Public Security Bureau for sentencing. In the afternoon, at around 2:00 PM, Director Wang opened the court and sentenced Zhou Runshi, Zhou Xingzhen, and Wang Yuhong (all prostitutes) to a fine of 15 yuan each according to the Law on Violations of Police Regulations. Wang Chongxi (former director of the Eighth Branch Bureau) was fined 30 yuan, Qin Enrui (former member of the Third Branch Bureau) was fined 15 yuan, and Jin Qiugen (room service in the New World Hotel, No. 83) was fined 15 yuan. After receiving the sentence, each person immediately paid the fine and was released. The case of the police inspector's prostitution has now been completely concluded.

Banning Illegal Shipping After the sinking of the Hengyi steamboat of the Taili Company in this town on the 14th of this month, which resulted in the drowning of ten passengers, most passengers are wary. The Suzhou Customs Supervisory Office believed that twelve steamboats from the Northeast Jisang and other steamboat companies in this town, such as Xiangyu and Xiangyuan, should have been repaired annually, but they had not yet sailed to the customs to comply with the regulations for re-inspection, which obviously intended to delay and posed a great danger to the lives and property of passengers. The office issued an order to the Construction Bureau of this town the day before to strictly ban each vessel in order to comply with the regulations. After receiving the order, Director Yao issued a notice to the steamship industry office yesterday, instructing each steamboat company to suspend operations immediately. Any violation is inconvenient.

Changzhou

The Postponement of the Opening of the Money Industry in the Market The Wuyi Commercial Market ended at the end of the lunar year, which was greatly affected by the rain and snow. Therefore, many industries were unable to settle accounts with the money industry as usual. Some money industries also failed to clear the Suzhou Zhuang accounts. For this reason, the money industry was hesitant to issue bills and conduct transactions for each industry. Some money shops themselves also had a small number of unsettled accounts. In previous years, the money industry would open on the fourth or fifth day of the lunar new year, but this year, due to the different circumstances, it was necessary to extend the time until the 26th of this month (the tenth day of the lunar year).

Fengxian

The Merger of the Two Pu and Qingcun Salt Fields The Song salt field has five fields: Yuanpu, Chongming, Xiasan, Qingcun, and Liangpu. After the Ministry of Finance sent personnel to investigate this time, it was considered that the situation of each field was vastly different from the past, and it was necessary to make changes. The three fields of Qingcun, Yuanpu, and Liangpu are not only geographically close but also have very similar products. The output of salt is less than that of farmland, and the affairs are particularly simple. Therefore, it was proposed to merge the Qingpu and Liangpu fields into the Yuanpu field in a moderate location for nearby management. A report has been submitted to the Ministry of Finance, and the field director, Li Yaonan, will be sent to take over separately. An official announcement was made yesterday that all affairs of the two fields will be directly under the jurisdiction of the field from this month onwards. However, the original collection offices of the field will be changed to branch counters for the convenience of the people to pay taxes and will be postponed for abolition.

Nantong

The Issue of Appeasement for the Lvsi Sea Bandits The sea bandits entrenched in the Lvsi area have undergone several internal conflicts. Recently, the remnant gang of Yan Zhendai, with over 300 bandits, requested appeasement from the district office, willing to clear the ocean surface of Yonghai and Qiru and hand over all their weapons. District Chief Cheng presented the request to the county government and forwarded it to the military and political authorities for approval.

The Re-establishment of Urban and Rural Telephone Lines The Nantong city telephone poles were broken by heavy snow, and the telephone lines were completely destroyed. Restoration is difficult. It has been decided to re-install the lines, which will take three months to restore telephone service.

The Difficulty of Handling the Upgrading of Reed Fields to Taxable Land The provincial government sent Jiang Yongyi to Nantong to handle the upgrading of reed fields to taxable land. After arriving in Nantong, Commissioner Jiang found that the registers were incomplete and there was no way to verify them. It was particularly difficult to make up for them. He specially reported to the province for instructions on how to proceed.

Zhenjiang

An Overview of the Closure of the Zhenjiang Commercial Market The accounts of all industries in the Zhenjiang commercial sector were closed on the 16th of this month. Traditionally, the money industry had the most surplus. Last year, due to the impact of the collapse of money shops in various counties in Jiangbei, the losses amounted to more than 1.1 million. Therefore, except for a few shops such as Yuan Yi, Yuan Sheng, and Heng Yuan, whose business conditions were different and not greatly affected, and had a surplus, the rest of the shops all suffered losses. Before the accounts were closed, the lack of silver dollars in Zhenjiang caused the shops to rampantly drive up prices, which greatly affected various industries. Later, the managers of Yuan Sheng and Dingchang shops transferred several million silver dollars from Shanghai to Zhenjiang to maintain the market and avoid huge losses. In addition, the foreign goods industry and the gold industry had a considerable surplus due to the increase in gold and pounds. As for the silk and cloth industry, the northern goods industry, the rice industry, the wood industry, and the tea industry, although there was not much surplus, they were generally stable.

Changshu

A Robbery and Kidnapping Case Discovered in Daqiao Town Daqiao Town, located in the western part of this county and bordering Jiangyin, is a small market town with dozens of households, none of which are very wealthy. At around 2:00 AM on the 18th of this month, more than 20 robbers, all armed with guns, first robbed the Wu Gengsheng family, taking away clothing and silver dollars. Then, they went to the neighboring Zhang Guisheng family (some say Lu), but Zhang was quite poor and had nothing of value to rob. This angered the robbers, who kidnapped Zhang, intending to demand a ransom. When they reached the vicinity of Majing Bridge, Zhang pleaded with the bandit leader to release him. The bandits, seeing his pitiful situation, released him. Later, they went to the Qian Sansi and Qian Genquan families in that area. Because the Qian family had sold rice last year and accumulated hundreds of silver dollars, all of these were taken away by the bandits, along with some valuable clothing. Sansi and Genquan were both injured when they resisted the bandits and have already gone to the hospital for treatment. Fortunately, their lives are not in danger. The total loss for the four families is estimated to be around a thousand gold.

Jiangyin

Zhu Xingnan Will Be Sent to the Commander-in-Chief's Headquarters Zhu Xingnan, a resident of Xiagang, was arrested in Suzhou and sent to the Zhenjiang Security Office in September last year for a reactionary case, and then transferred to the Temporary Military Law Joint Trial Office. He has been suffering from a severe illness in detention recently. His abandoned wife, Shen Yunzhen, requested the Security Office to release him on bail for medical treatment. The reply was that the case was ordered by the Commander-in-Chief's Headquarters to be sent to Beijing for interrogation, and the request for bail for medical treatment could not be approved. He should be treated properly before being sent on the journey.

Establishment of Confidential Report Boxes in the Four Cities The First District Office received an order from the county government to establish confidential report boxes in its jurisdiction in accordance with the resolution of the Defense Conference, to collect information. The boxes will be opened and closed by the district chief himself. If there are any confidential reports, the district chief should immediately work with the police and militia to handle them properly. After receiving the order, District Chief Zhu set up the boxes in the four cities yesterday.

Inquiring about the Method for the Remaining Prisoner Food and Funds The county government received an order from the High Court the day before, stating that Jiangyin was allocated 30 prisoners' food rations for convicts whose cases had been concluded, which would be paid from the judicial expenses. The remaining expenses should be managed by the county separately. County Magistrate Li ordered the Property Department to find a way to do so under the local expenses. Chief Zhang believed that banditry was rampant in this county, and there were often 100 to 200 people detained. If all the remaining prisoner food rations were to be managed under the local expenses, it would be difficult to find a way to do so, regardless of whether the funds were exhausted. It would also be difficult to achieve fairness in terms of reason and emotion. However, since the matter concerned a provincial order, yesterday he specially inquired about the methods used by the Property Departments of Wuxi, Wujin, Changshu, Nantong, Liyang, Yixing, Rugao, and other counties for reference.

Gaoyou

The Judgment on the Case of Enticement between the Boss's Wife and the Apprentice Zhu Ziliang, the manager of Shenchang Company outside the South Gate of this city, previously filed a lawsuit with the county government against his wife, Wang, and the apprentice, Xue Shaotang, for enticement. It is now heard that the county government has already rendered a judgment. The judgment is as follows: It was learned that Xue Shaotang had previously served as an apprentice at Shenchang Company. Zhu Ziliang was usually on bad terms with his wife, Wang. As a result, Wang went out with Guo, a waiter at the Dingxin Inn, and fled to Xue Shaotang's house. Zhu Ziliang then filed a complaint with the government on the charge of enticement. After the government summoned witnesses for interrogation, the portion on enticement was vehemently denied not only by Zhu, Wang, and Xue Shaotang, but also by their daughter, Zhu Chunyin, who testified that her father beat her mother for buying a small amount of opium. Xue Shaotang had never been to our house in Gaoyou, nor had he talked to my mother at the inn. Furthermore, Xue Shaotang has a wife at home. If Zhu Wang and he were having an affair, why wouldn't they live separately? How dare they openly go to his house with Guo? Therefore, it is clear that Zhu Wang and Xue Shaotang's adultery is untrue. As for the portion on enticement, the criminal law does not explicitly punish women over the age of twenty. Moreover, Zhu Wang is already thirty-eight years old. Regardless of whether there was enticement or not, since there is no punitive provision in the criminal law, there is no crime to speak of. Based on the above analysis, the criminal suspicion of the defendants is insufficient and they should not be prosecuted in accordance with Article 244, Section 2 of the Criminal Procedure Law.

Ningbo

A Compilation of Robbery Cases (1) The Zunshu Temple in Chenye, East Township of Yin County, which housed seven nuns, was suddenly visited by five robbers last night. Speaking with a Taiwanese accent, they used large stones to break down the door and enter, robbing 44 silver dollars, 16 small silver coins, one gold ring, and five cotton quilts, causing a loss of over 200 gold. (2) At the home of Xu Abiao, a resident of Guojiafenzhuang, East Township of Yin County, five robbers suddenly arrived at 12:00 AM the night before, robbing 87 silver dollars and valuable items, causing a loss of over 100 yuan. (3) Zheng Afu, a farmer from Qinong, Fifth Township of Yin County, went to the city to buy goods the day before. While passing the pavilion near the Huacheng Nunnery in that area, he suddenly encountered three robbers. One robber slashed Afu's leg twice, causing Afu to faint and fall to the ground. Another robber immediately undressed him and searched him, robbing 25 French dollars and over 10 yuan of southern goods before fleeing. (4) At the home of Yu Zhoushi, a resident of Yang, Xiangshan, multiple robbers suddenly arrived at midnight on the 18th of this month. Each held土 guns, wooden clubs, and other items, breaking into the room and

looting all the clothing and other items. They also demanded silver dollars but failed and stabbed Zhoushi before leaving.

Letters to the Editor

Letter from Changshu County Government

Dear Editor, We have reviewed the "National Important News" column in your newspaper on January 28th of this year, which contains a special dispatch from Jiangyin stating that a reconnaissance team discovered a土 boat with hundreds of catties of 土 in Shanquan Lake in our county. We immediately sent a letter to the Jiangyin County Government to inquire about the actual situation. We have now received a reply, which indicates that it was a matter of dumping soil in the Rongdu port within the Jiangyin boundary, which is inconsistent with the facts stated in your newspaper. We hope that you will publish this letter in the "Letters to the Editor" section to clarify the truth. Respectfully, Changshu County Government, February 19th.

Yesterday's Westerners' Football Match: Shanghai True Joy Great Victory

▲ Seven to Three Victory over the Lancers

丨Returning from the Philippines, Remaining Courage is Laudable丨

The sound of firecrackers shook the ears, and the cheers shook the sky. This was the scene yesterday at the Shanghai Garden, where five thousand spectators welcomed the True Joy team, who had just returned from their expedition and achieved another victory over the Lancers. The True Joy athletes were also overwhelmed by the favor and ecstatic with joy. They should strive even harder, make efforts to improve, and not disappoint the ardent expectations of the people.

▲ Seven to Three, the Enemy Turned Downwind

The True Joy team returned after a long absence, full of heroic spirit. The Lancers, rested and ready, were full of energy. A great battle was inevitable. With a simple effort, True Joy scored three consecutive goals. The audience raised their eyebrows in triumph, danced and cheered. But extreme joy breeds sorrow, and prosperity turns to decline. Within five minutes, they lost two goals. The players stepped up their efforts, and the audience shouted encouragement. In the blink of an eye, they scored two more goals in quick succession. Near the end of the game, the Lancers regained a goal. In the first half, True Joy took the lead with five goals to three. In the second half, True Joy, riding the momentum of their victory, soon broke through the enemy's defenses repeatedly, scoring two more goals. As the battle closed, True Joy won with seven goals to three.

▲ The New Lineup's Strength is Astonishing

The change in True Joy after their Philippine expedition was the alteration of their lineup. In the past, Chen Zhenhe occupied a pivotal central position, responding to all directions. Now, he is listed at the forefront, charging into battle. Chen Jiaqiu was transferred back to the interior, changing from attack to defense, each in their proper place, suitable for both attack and defense. This move greatly improved the overall strength of the team. However, Xie Quanhe's goalkeeping is more than strong, but his intelligence and experience are still not as good as Liang Guanlian's. Yang Baosen is a promising newcomer, and his future is bright. As for the skills of the other warriors, the audience has long formed their own opinions, so there is no need to elaborate.

War Clouds Rise, the Enemy Strikes First

At three o'clock, the war clouds were thick, and the enemy struck first. The ball came from the left, crossed in front of the goal, and returned to the center from the right wing. The left inside forward shot, but the ball was weak. Goalkeeper Xie Quanhe caught it and threw it out. The ball came to the goal again, and the goalkeeper dove to the ground to save it, showing considerable skill. It then turned into a corner kick. The shot was very good, but it was headed away without success. After several waves, they were avoided one by one. As the clouds broke and the moon appeared, after hardship comes happiness. Our warriors were preparing their equipment, waiting for the opportunity to move.

▲ Five Tiger Generals Break Through the Enemy's Fortress Three Times

The Lancers' attack was ineffective, and their defense was improper. Within the penalty area, the five tiger generals of True Joy could be seen relying on their skills, colliding left and right. Fu, on the left wing, made an accurate cross. Dai Zhongge took advantage of the situation and deflected the ball diagonally. Luo Haiguang seized the opportunity and scored a goal. Yang Bao, the main kicker, took a free kick. Luo Haiguang turned his foot to the right, and Chen Zhenhe fearlessly jumped up and headed the ball into the net. Mei, on the right wing, embarked on a long expedition. Chen Zhenhe asked for a pass, and the ball came to the goal. Luo Haiguang was blessed with a rare opportunity and reaped great success. The three goals were scored within fifteen minutes, averaging one goal every five minutes.

▲ Striving to be First, Both Sides Work Hard Together

Under pressure, the enemy worked hard to counterattack. The left wing chipped the ball in, and inside right Ke Laituo took the opportunity to shoot, cutting into the goal. In the blink of an eye, right wing Mite penetrated deep into the hinterland, turned his foot and passed to the left. Left wing Aierjie met it with a kick. The goalkeeper got it but still lost it. The Lancers, in one go, scored two consecutive goals, causing the audience to feel uneasy. However, the True Joy athletes were full of courage. A little setback did not dampen their spirits. At first, they took advantage of the enemy's absence and the emptiness inside. Dai, the center forward, took the lead and attacked the goal on his own. The goalkeeper was caught off guard, rushed forward to compete, and was tricked into falling to the ground. Defender Mite quickly returned to defend, and Dai, the center forward, shot fiercely. Mite was flustered and let it into the net. Subsequently, Mei, on the right wing, kicked a corner kick, and Dai, the center forward, headed it in successfully, making the score five to two. As time was about to run out, Lancers' Ke Laituo scored a goal in a melee. In the first half, True Joy took the lead with five to three.

In the second half, with renewed cheers, True Joy was full of vigor and energy, and the forwards pressed on relentlessly. Yang Baosen passed the ball to the left, but Luo Haiguang, being watched, deliberately avoided it. Fu He quickened his pace, faked a shot, and angled the ball into the net. From then on, True Joy shot high and low, back and forth endlessly. Dai, the center forward, received the ball from Mei, the right wing, and casually sent it in, making it the final score of seven to three for the day. In the following thirty-five minutes, although True Joy's momentum was strong, scoring was difficult. This was because the enemy worked hard to defend in order to avoid the shame of losing ground and humiliating their team again.

The Shanghai Basketball Association Committee held a temporary meeting at the Deng Tuomo Hotel on Sichuan Road at 12 noon yesterday. All members attended, discussing various issues related to this year's International Basketball Tournament and League. The meeting lasted for three hours before adjourning. The records are as follows:

(1) Because the Wu team was unable to attend on time due to office hours and traffic delays, and the game with Black Star was a past event, but because the competition rules of the association could not be easily accommodated, a letter of explanation and comfort should be sent.

(2) In the game between Huadong and the team on February 18, Lu Zhongen, a player of the Huadong team, deliberately threw the ball at the opponent's backboard to mock the enemy, and people in the team (non-players) went to the field to persuade the players to stop the game. A losers' tournament will be prepared for teams without final rights to join. For women, the competition method will be determined based on the number of registered teams.

The National Government Issues This Year's National Games Competition Regulations

▲ Government Instruction

National Government Instruction No. 96, February 19th, 20th year [of the Republic], instructs the Executive Yuan: For matters of instruction, the Preparatory Committee of the National Games of the 20th year of the Republic submits, for approval and record, the competition regulations of the National Games of the 20th year of the Republic, and instructs all provinces, cities, districts, and overseas Chinese organizations to comply accordingly. Having examined the date and location of the National Games, the committee has submitted them to the government for review and record, and has issued orders accordingly. All competition regulations prior to the opening date should also be determined as soon as possible, so that all participating organizations can prepare and avoid future disputes. In view of this, the committee has hired domestic sports experts, referring to the rules of the Far Eastern Games and the World Games, to carefully draft 34 articles of the National Games competition regulations. They have also been carefully reviewed and finalized by the 11th committee meeting of the committee. Therefore, this document, together with 200 copies of the regulations, is submitted to the government for approval and record, and is requested to be issued to all provinces, cities, districts, and overseas Chinese organizations for compliance, which is truly convenient, etc. Based on this, in addition to instructing that the submitted documents be fully understood and approved for record, the Executive Yuan is requested to send them to the Central Overseas Chinese Affairs Commission for separate implementation. This instruction, along with the issuance and distribution, includes 150 copies of the original regulations, instructing the Executive Yuan to order compliance. This instruction includes 150 copies of the regulations issued. Chairman Chiang Chung-cheng, Premier of the Executive Yuan Chiang Chung-cheng.

▲ Competition Regulations

Chapter 1: Date and Location

Article 1: The Games are scheduled to be held from October 10th to October 20th, 20th year of the Republic, at the Central Sports Field in the capital. If necessary, the Games Committee may decide to extend it.

Chapter 2: Competition Units

Article 2: All championship competitions shall be based on the following provinces, cities, districts, and overseas Chinese organizations as units:

(1) Provinces: Jiangsu, Zhejiang, Anhui, Jiangxi, Hunan, Hubei, Sichuan, Xi, Fujian, Guangdong, Guangxi, Guizhou, Yunnan, Shandong, Henan, Hebei, Shanxi, Shaanxi, Gansu, Ningxia, Liaoning, Jilin, Heilongjiang, Qiaoyuan, Rehe, Chahar, Xinjiang, Qinghai, Tibet, and Mongolia.

(2) Cities: Nanjing, Shanghai, Qingdao, Tianjin, Hankou

(3) Districts: Hong Kong, Harbin

(4) Overseas Chinese Organizations: Java, Honolulu, the Philippines, and other overseas Chinese organizations.

Chapter 3: Athlete Eligibility

Article 3: All citizens of the Republic of China may be selected to represent their local unit and attend the Games, but must not violate the following two provisions:

(1) Athletes must be amateur athletes (amateur sports rules will be determined separately).

(2) Each athlete shall not represent two or more units at the same time.

Chapter 4: Types of Championships

Article 4: The types of championships set up for the Games competition are as follows:

(1) Men's Division: Track and Field Championship, Running Championship, All-Around Championship, Swimming Championship, Soccer Championship, Basketball Championship, Tennis Championship, Volleyball Championship, Baseball Championship

(2) Women's Division: Track and Field Championship, Swimming Championship, Basketball Championship, Tennis Championship, Volleyball Championship

(3) National Arts Division: Chinese Wrestling Championship, Fencing Championship, Pugilism Championship

Chapter 5: Sports Events

Article 5: The sports events included in the Track and Field, Running, All-Around, and Swimming Championships are as follows:

(1) Track and Field:

(A) Men's Track and Field: High Jump, Pole Vault, Long Jump, Triple Jump, Shot Put (16 lbs), Discus Throw, Javelin Throw

(B) Men's Running: 100m, 200m, 400m, 800m, 1500m, 10000m, 110m Hurdles, 400m Hurdles

(C) Women's Track and Field: High Jump, Long Jump, Javelin Throw, Shot Put (8 lbs), 50m, 100m, 200m, 4x100m Relay, 80m Hurdles

(2) All-Around:

(A) Pentathlon: Long Jump, Javelin Throw, 200m, Discus Throw, 1500m

(B) Decathlon: 100m, Long Jump, Shot Put (16 lbs), High Jump, 400m, 110m Hurdles, Discus Throw, Pole Vault, Javelin Throw, 1500m

(C) 4x100m Relay

(D) 4x400m Relay

(3) Swimming:

(A) Men's: 50m Freestyle, 100m Freestyle, 100m Backstroke, 200m Breaststroke, 400m Freestyle, 1500m Freestyle, 4x200m Freestyle Relay, Diving Competition

(B) Women's: 50m Freestyle, 100m Freestyle, 100m Backstroke, 200m Breaststroke, 4x200m Freestyle Relay

Chapter 6: Competition Rules

Article 6: The competition rules for all championship competitions shall be handled in accordance with the rules jointly approved by the Games and the China National Amateur Athletic Federation. However, the competition rules for all National Arts competitions shall be handled in accordance with the rules jointly approved by the Games and the Central National Arts Institute.

Chapter 7: Methods of Winning Championships

Article 7: The competition methods for each championship are as follows:

(1) Competition: For running, all-around, and swimming, the unit with the most points wins the championship. If two or more units have the same score, the unit with the most first-place finishes wins the championship. If the number of first-place finishes is equal, then the number of second-place finishes will be used to determine the winner, and so on.

(2) For all types of ball championships, the knockout system will be used, and the winner of the final will be the champion. If the outcome of the final is undecided, the time should be extended or a replay should be held in accordance with the rules.

Chapter 8: Overall Championship

Article 8: The Games' overall championship is divided into male and female categories, each awarded to the unit with the most championships (excluding the National Arts Championship). If two or more units have the same number of championships, the total score of the track and field championships of that unit will be used to determine the winner. If the scores are equal, the provisions of Article 7, paragraph 1 of these regulations shall apply.

Chapter 9: Participation Methods

Article 9: Each unit should handle participation matters through the Education Bureau and the National Arts Institute. Ball teams, National Arts teams, or athletes shall not register directly with the Games in their individual names.

Article 10: Units without an Education Bureau or National Arts Institute may designate a responsible organization in that unit to contact the Games for handling.

Article 11: Each unit should, before September 10th, telegraph the Games the types of championships they intend to participate in, in order to prepare the schedule. Late submissions will be invalid.

Article 12: Each unit should, before September 25th, send the full list of athletes to the Games by telegram or registered mail. If it is necessary to change the list of athletes, it should be notified to the Games before October 3rd. No further changes will be allowed after the deadline.

Article 13: The list of athletes must be filled out using the forms printed by the Games, in ink. Those who use their own paper or write unclearly will be considered invalid.

Article 14: All incoming and outgoing mail and telegrams must indicate the date for verification.

Chapter 10: Athlete Quota

Article 15: The number of athletes participating in each championship competition in each unit shall not exceed the following regulations:

1. Track and Field and Swimming: Each unit may add four athletes to each event. Each athlete may participate in up to four events, male and female alike.

2. All-Around: Each unit may add six athletes to each event, but athletes may not participate in both the pentathlon and the decathlon at the same time.

3. Soccer: Each team shall have a maximum of 15 players.

4. Basketball: Each men's team shall have a maximum of 10 players, and each women's team shall have a maximum of 12 players.

5. Tennis: Each team shall have a maximum of 4 players, male and female alike.

6. Volleyball: Each men's team shall have a maximum of 12 players, and each women's team shall have a maximum of 15 players.

7. Baseball: Each team shall have a maximum of 15 players.

8. National Arts: Each competition shall have a maximum of four athletes per team. Each unit may only add one team to each championship.

Chapter 11: Leader and Instructor Quota

Article 16: Each unit shall have one overall leader responsible for all contacts and discussions.

Article 17: Each team may have one instructor and one manager each.

Chapter 12: Competition Protests

Article 18: Protests regarding a certain competition shall be formally submitted in writing to the Judging Committee by the overall leader of each unit or its representative within one hour after the conclusion of the competition.

Article 19: After receiving the protest, the Judging Committee shall convene a meeting to resolve it as soon as possible. The judgment shall be final.

Article 20: A deposit of ten yuan shall be attached to the protest. If the Judging Committee considers the protest to be unfounded, the deposit may be confiscated.

Chapter 13: Eligibility Protests

Article 21: Protests regarding athletes violating amateur regulations shall be submitted to the Judging Committee for resolution in accordance with the procedures specified in Chapter 12 of these regulations.

Article 22: If the aforementioned protest is filed before the competition, the Judging Committee shall immediately convene a meeting to resolve it. The judgment shall be final.

Article 23: If the aforementioned protest occurs during the competition, it shall be submitted to the Judging Committee within one hour after the end of the competition.

Article 24: Athletes participating in track and field, all-around, swimming, and National Arts who have been confirmed to have violated amateur regulations shall have their individual qualifications and their scores canceled.

Article 25: If any unit in a ball championship competition uses a non-amateur athlete as a player to participate in the competition, once confirmed, the qualification of that unit in that championship competition shall be canceled.

Article 26: Athletes or teams whose qualifications have been canceled due to violation of amateur eligibility shall have all prizes and certificates recovered.

Chapter 14: Prizes

Article 27: The Games prizes are divided into team and individual categories. Individual prizes include a certificate in addition to a medal.

Article 28: All championship teams will be given a team prize. Second, third, and fourth place in track and field, all-around, swimming, and National Arts will also be given a team prize. The prizes are silver cups or banks.

Article 29: The top four winning athletes in track and field, all-around, swimming, and National Arts championship competitions will be given individual prizes. The distribution is as follows:

First Place: Gold medal and certificate

Second Place: Silver medal and certificate

Third Place: Bronze medal and certificate

Fourth Place: White bronze medal and certificate

Article 30: All members of ball championship teams will be given gold medals and certificates.

Article 31: The Games' overall championship for men and women will be awarded a large silver cauldron each.

Article 32: Athletes who create new national records may be submitted by the Competition Committee to the Games for special awards separately to encourage them.

Chapter 15: Travel Expenses and Accommodation

Article 33: The travel expenses and meals for athletes, instructors, managers, leaders, etc. participating in the Games from each unit shall be borne by each unit. The accommodation will be prepared by the Games.

Article 34: Except for athletes, instructors, managers, leaders, and those invited by the Games, no one will be entertained.

Anecdotes of Wumen: Old Man Who Feeds Cattle

▲ Extraordinary Cold with Heavy Snow. This year, the 20th day of the 11th month of Gengwu was extraordinarily cold. According to this newspaper, it was unprecedented in more than 30 years. Recalling that in the early November of the 19th year of Guangxu (Renchen), heavy snow fell for five days and nights. The accumulated snow was more than a foot deep on the ground. Plank houses and thatched huts, both inside and outside the city, were all toppled. The cold was below zero degrees Celsius. The bottom of Taihu Lake was frozen solid. From Wan'nian Bridge at Xumen to Hengtang Yuelaixi, vehicles and horses traveled on it. Countless boats in the lake were shattered by the ice. Ice pillars hung from the eaves of people's houses, like bamboo poles from the corners of the roof to the ground. Children knocked them down to make bamboo horses to ride. Most of the poor and beggars froze to death. Coffins were sold out, and large porcelain jars were used for burial. The strangest thing was that barbershops shaved beards for people. As soon as a knife fell, the skin and beard came off together, leading to lawsuits in court. The whole city laughed about it. People who are now 60 years old can still talk about it. I was 19 years old at that time. In a blink of an eye, I am old. In the blink of an eye, I have reached the 甲戍 sixty years. Extraordinary cold has been encountered twice. The cold of Renchen lasted about half a month, while the cold of Gengwu only lasted one day.

▲ Tang Wenzheng Destroys the Five Saints Temple. The Five Tong Gods in the south are like the fox spirits in the north. Their tracks are erratic. Once a god comes down, it cannot be driven away. Zhijin Mountain outside Qimen in Suzhou, commonly known as Shangfang Mountain. The pagoda courtyard enshrines the Five Saints. According to legend, the Five Saints are five brothers. The residents at the foot of the mountain call them the Great Lord, Second Lord, Third Lord, Fourth Lord, and Fifth Lord. The Third Lord is the most powerful, with clear rewards and punishments. In the areas of Hengtang, Lishi, and Xinguoli around the mountain, young women in rural villages are often secretly defiled by the Five Saints. Once defiled, their families will be rewarded. The poor will become well-off immediately. If they are defiled and unwilling to submit, and they hire monks and Taoists to set up altars to worship Buddha to suppress them, they will be severely punished, either by fire or disease. Therefore, they dare to be angry but dare not speak out and listen to the ravages. Every year on the 17th and 18th nights of August, the Xingchun Bridge has flutes and drums, painted boats, thousands of lights and candles. The whole city is empty and alleys are cleared to climb the mountain to offer sacrifices. It is common practice. The official government does not prohibit it. Even if it is prohibited, there is nothing that can be done. In the early years of Kangxi, Mr. Tang Jie'an (Bin) of Suizhou was the Governor of Jiangnan.

Yuzhou · 7 · 5 · Old Man

I happened to read in Fang Yu Ji Yao that Yuzhou Mountain is 19 miles northeast of Haizhou, in the sea. There is a large continent surrounded by hundreds of miles, called Yuzhou, also known as Yuzhou. The Shan Hai Jing calls it Yu Mountain in the sea. In the fifth year of Jin Long'an, Sun En attacked Jiankang, but failed and fled north across the sea to Yuzhou, and so on. In the 20th century, finding land for colonization is the only policy of various countries. Yuzhou is close to the sea border. In the event of war, it is deeply worried that it will be occupied by the enemy as a place for shelter, water extraction, and colonization. This is even more important than Hong Kong and other places next to the bed. I don't know what the situation is there now. My old eyes are dim and the maps are small. I was unable to find out when I was a child, and I don't know if the naval community has paid attention to it.

A Thought · Autumn · Water

▲ If an old man marries a young woman, people will envy or be jealous. If an old woman marries a young man, people will mock her. Such is the inequality between men and women.

▲ God put vanity in the minds of men so that women could conquer, soften, and civilize them.

▲ A man's love is as worthless as a year-old calendar, unless you can possess all of it.

▲ Love is like the hair on your head and the teeth in your mouth. When you have it, it is priceless; when you lose it, it is not worth half a penny.

▲ Modern marriage is like a modern novel, getting shorter every day. When you stand under the wedding altar, listening to the pastor's mumbling words, you can turn to the last page and see the final result.

▲ Almost every woman can marry a man if the latter can manage to forget his former woman. A man who feels ashamed in this situation shows his weakness.

▲ A capable man issues commands at home like gentle advice. A smart woman issues commands to men like a sweet request.

▲ Love is a red carrot that lures stupid men, like donkeys, to abandon the free wilderness and enter a trap.

It is said that there are evil gods and lewd sacrifices in Suzhou. As soon as he got out of the car, he immediately led his soldiers and informed the military, civilians, and all kinds of people to go to the top of Shangfang Mountain together, burn down the temple, and throw the clay statues of the Five Saints into Taihu Lake. From then on, the women in the neighborhoods could protect their chastity, and the people of the nine counties praised him with their hands on their foreheads, saying that Ximen Bao's governance of witchcraft did not have such virtue. So they donated money to collect stones and built a memorial archway next to the Xuguan Reception Pavilion, with the four characters "The People Cannot Forget" inscribed on it. Officials passing by in boats and carriages all looked up and contemplated, and after three hundred years, the story is still told.

Fragments of the Guangji Steamer Breaking the Bandits · Perilous Heart

The situation of the China Merchants Bureau's Guangji steamer encountering pirates and being damaged has already been reported in the newspapers. However, Mr. Li, a passenger on the steamer when it arrived in Shanghai, told me many noteworthy details, which I am eager to recount for public viewing.

▲ Handsome Bandit Leader The bandit leader, Ye Mingsheng, is only twenty-six years old, with a handsome face, looking like a nobleman's son. He was wearing a dark-colored camel hair robe. When he boarded the ship, he booked cabin number nine, a first-class cabin. The crew members saw that he was carrying a large leather bag and occupying the cabin alone, and suspected that he was an important person in the party, so they treated him very well. Unexpectedly, after the ship sailed, the bandit leader went to the steerage cabin to observe the wealth of the passengers. He lingered near passengers with a lot of luggage. He also made gestures and eye contact with a dozen or so people wearing blue cloth clothes, belted at the waist, and wearing felt hats. This aroused great suspicion among the crew members. When they reported to the Chao Wu warship's water police at Huanghua Pass for investigation, the case was solved.

▲ Oil-Soaked Hemp Rope When the bandit leader was arrested and taken to the Chao Wu warship, he stubbornly refused to confess. The captain took a hemp rope soaked in tung oil and whipped him hard. First, he asked if the Xin Ning Tai steamer had been robbed by him. At this point, the bandit could not bear the pain and had to confess the truth.

▲ Robbery Plan The bandit confessed the details of the robbery, saying that he was from Haimen and was publicly elected by the Tai bandits as the leader for handling affairs abroad (i.e., the robbery boss). The Xin Ning Tai steamer was also robbed by the Tai bandits, but he was not in command. This time, they planned to rob the Guangji. The bandits considered it many times and designated 140 people to handle the case. Twenty people boarded the ship, and 120 people were sent to drive six bandit ships to wait on the sea surface 100 miles outside Huanghua Pass, preparing to move the stolen goods. He had an agency in Wenzhou. This time he boarded the ship to rob 300,000 yuan. If the ship did not have enough money, they would rob the Guangji steamer and order the China Merchants Bureau to redeem it for 300,000 yuan, because the Guangji had a shallow draft and a small hull, so it could be robbed into various straits.

▲ Fortunes of Each Ship The bandit leader, Ye Mingsheng, also said that the gang planned to rob merchant ships, starting with the Guangji steamer. After that, they decided to rob the Xin Bao Shan Da Xing Yi Li Zhou Shan and Chuan Shan six ships on the Shanghai-Taiwan line one by one. They planned to rob seven ships within two months. Now that he had been arrested, the plan to rob the ships had been broken. It was fortunate for the various shipping bureaus, especially the China Merchants Bureau. He also said that there were six or seven hundred bandits in the same party, scattered on the coastal islands, with agencies in Shanghai and Wenzhou.

▲ Easy Robbery and Escort to Wenzhou There is a bandit agency in the East Gate of Wenzhou, and the bandit leader was also captured. However, Ye had been severely tortured and his legs were broken, so he could not move. So they changed to the third bandit leader to Ou. A base was uncovered in the East Gate, and the four bandits who stayed in Wenzhou had already fled, and only one wooden-cased gun was found. Now the bandits have been escorted back to the Chao Wu warship, and the captain is investigating the location of their bandit dens in order to send a large team of military police to suppress them and rescue the kidnapped passengers of the Xin Ning Tai steamer.

Trivial Talks on Westerners Studying Chinese Literature · Laughing Shanghai

The other night, I happened to talk to my elders about Westerners studying Chinese literature, which was quite interesting. But we Chinese seem to feel ashamed of it.

During the late Qing Dynasty, there was an American named Ding Huizhen who was extremely fond of studying Chinese literature. He was familiar with all the classics, histories, philosophies, and collections. During the Guangxu period, he was even selected as a Hanlin scholar in our country, which was also considered strange. Ding once had a couplet, soliciting responses from our Chinese people. The couplet was "One three birds harm people: crows, pigeons, sparrows." The meaning was the opium in our country, the black curtain of releasing white pigeons in society, and the mahjong tiles (three things), the content contains eating, prostituting, gambling three things. ) The content includes eating, whoring, and gambling, which are very harmful to people. When the Chinese people saw that his first line had been written, they searched their brains and conceived a second line. Before long, one person came up with it and wrote to Ding. The second line was "Four things eliminate you: scales, phoenixes, dragons." Ding read it and was furious, because there was an ancient saying in our country: "Scales, phoenixes, dragons, turtles." This was probably satirizing Ding as a turtle. Ding then came up with another couplet, cursing the Chinese people, saying, "Sparrow top, horseshoe sleeves, dressed as animals." The meaning was scolding the Qing people's clothing. But until now, no one has been able to come up with a matching line. (Note: This Ding Huizhen was the one who drafted the treaty during the Eight-Nation Alliance.)

When the Shanghai International Settlement Mixed Court had not been taken back, a foreign assessor in the court was well-versed in the Four Books. During the May 30th Massacre, several university students went to see the foreigner. The foreigner questioned them with the teachings of Confucius. The university students all stared blankly and could not answer. After a long time, they finally said, "The books believed by the Confucian scholars are not applicable to the present era." The foreigner smiled and said, "Don't say it's not applicable. This kind of doctrine is immortal. I hope you will read it carefully." The university students all retreated in shame.

Tragic News of the Zhejiang Epidemic · Shi Yan Ye

Since the beginning of the year, the epidemic in Zhejiang has been rampant. Unfortunately, thousands of people have died of meningitis. It is truly a great disaster for the people of Zhejiang in the past twenty years. A friend from Zhejiang came to Shanghai and told me two very tragic stories from the epidemic. I wrote them down to share in this discussion.

▲ Groom Dies of Epidemic, Bride Becomes a Nun In the village of Zhuji, a relative of my friend, surnamed Tian, married a woman surnamed Song ten days after New Year's Day. Guests and friends gathered, and joy overflowed the courtyard. The newlyweds were originally united to fight against the harsh environment, so they felt even more proud and ambitious on this day. Unexpectedly, joy was just beginning, and tragedy followed. Soon after the auspicious day, the groom suddenly contracted the epidemic. In the remote rural area, medicine was hard to come by in times of need. The local doctors who were called in were all outsiders to this disease and could not prescribe the right medicine. Sadly, before the day was over, the groom abandoned his lover and left. The groom's two old parents wept bitterly for their beloved son, needless to say. The bride was even more distraught and wanted to die. When her husband's coffin was placed in the hall, she repeatedly wanted to jump in and become a pair of mandarin ducks in the afterlife, but she was prevented by many people. After the incident, she took poison, but was discovered by someone. Five days later, she took the opportunity to go to Hangzhou and had her head shaved in a temple. When her family on both sides found her, they cried and begged her to return, but she refused. She said that if she returned, she would vow to die. Staying here would still give her hope of seeing them again. She begged them not to go against her will to live a stolen life. Seeing that her will could not be taken away, they agreed. From then on, a thin-fated beauty was added between the Six Bridges and the Three Tianzhu Temples, spending her days listening to the morning bell and evening drum. Alas.

▲ Beloved Son Dies Tragically, Father Follows In a town near Hangzhou, an old man surnamed Huang had a son at the age of sixty. His family fortune was in the hundreds of thousands. The old man was satisfied that his great wealth would have a son to inherit it. But Heaven was not kind and brought misfortune to this five-year-old son. The lively and innocent child died of illness in less than three hours. Even great wealth could not redeem the life of the child. The old man lost this treasure and felt hopeless about the future. His old and frail body grieved several times and then he lay in bed. His broken heart could not be saved by medicine. Eight days after his beloved son died tragically, the old father followed him and left. It was also tragic.
